function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 429') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.429!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php') != '00f7fe6139131e73a510adf8e22f5f4090c90e7f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php') !== '00f7fe6139131e73a510adf8e22f5f4090c90e7f') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php') !== '93dea3f52d33ad27d4901e1a688967cf68493329') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php') !== '00f7fe6139131e73a510adf8e22f5f4090c90e7f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusRA.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '674a75456c56deef5199a20670a210a31ea74173') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '674a75456c56deef5199a20670a210a31ea74173') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '856a849f4498cf7ca7b027eb431a6d435549734f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '674a75456c56deef5199a20670a210a31ea74173') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
